 26 november, 2008 ko mumbai main hue aatanki hamale main 166 log maare gaye the
 "it is clear in the article that the terror attack was carried out by non-governmental elements against whom the Federal Investigation Agency (FIA) conducted a thorough professional investigation and which is being prosecuted by the Government of Pakistan," Khosa said
 khosa ne kaha ki sajeesh kaa maamla sabit karne kii jatiltaaon ko unke peshewar nazariye ke taur par dikhaaya gaya tha

 Khosa said that the complexities of proving a conspiracy case were shown in his professional view
